                - paragraph [ref=e215]: Adaptive lessons
                - heading "Clinical depth without the textbook fog." [level=2] [ref=e216]
                - paragraph [ref=e217]: "The lesson model is built around how nurses actually think at the bedside: recognize the pattern, decide what matters, act safely, and explain why."
                - generic [ref=e218]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e219]: Priority cue
                  - paragraph [ref=e220]: A patient with heart failure, new crackles, and falling oxygen saturation needs rapid respiratory assessment before routine discharge teaching.
              - generic [ref=e221]:
                - article [ref=e222]:
                  - img [ref=e224]
                  - heading "Pathophysiology" [level=3] [ref=e226]
                  - paragraph [ref=e227]: "Start with the why: preload, afterload, gas exchange, perfusion, and compensatory cues before memorizing interventions."
                - article [ref=e228]:
                  - img [ref=e230]
                  - heading "Labs and diagnostics" [level=3] [ref=e232]
                  - paragraph [ref=e233]: Connect ABGs, electrolytes, cardiac markers, cultures, and imaging clues to the next safest nursing action.
                - article [ref=e234]:
                  - img [ref=e236]

                  - img [ref=e242]

                  - img [ref=e250]

# Test source

  33  | function shardAllows(name: string): boolean {
  34  |   const s = process.env.E2E_REGRESSION_SHARD?.trim();
  35  |   if (!s || s === "all") return true;
  36  |   const seoMarketing = ["seo-marketing-sample", "screenshot-matrix"];
  37  |   const learnerGuest = ["guest-cat-ecg-labs-probes", "locale-theme-footer"];
  38  |   if (s === "1") return seoMarketing.includes(name);
  39  |   if (s === "2") return learnerGuest.includes(name);
  40  |   return true;
  41  | }
